Song Ziwen

Talking About Impressions of the Trip to Shandong 131

Meeting with Key Figures Without Formal Discussions on Official Business

Shandong Province's Production is Developing and Construction is Advancing

Dredging of Xiaoqing River Will Be Proposed at Water Conservancy Conference

Denying the Rumor that the Economic Commission Controls Grain

Song Ziwen, a standing committee member of the National Economic Commission, returned south from Qingdao to Jinan and arrived in Beijing the morning before yesterday. He then took a special express train back to Shanghai at 5 p.m. He arrived at the wharf at 11:30 p.m. and got off the train at the Zhenru Station. Yesterday morning at 11 a.m., he met with reporters from various newspapers at the Shanghai office of the Economic Commission on West Xiangsi Road to talk about the trip. The following is a summary of his conversation.

Shandong Province's Agricultural Production Bumper Harvest This Year 132

Song Ziwen first said that he was invited by Chairman Han (Fuqu) to study the province's economic plan. After inspecting Qingdao and Jinan, he learned that Shandong had a very good harvest this year. Cotton and wheat production was very strong, and peanut production was even more abundant. Now, we are further promoting sales and transporting them to Guangdong and other provinces, which has led to higher selling prices.

Jinan Textile Mill Can Actually Make a Profit 133

Especially the textile mills in Jinan left the best impression on me. Two of them use the latest machines, the 1933 and 1934 models, which makes their production capacity very strong. Another factory uses machines that are partly made by the factory itself, and the required price can be reduced by more than two-thirds compared with imported products. In addition, the workers in Shandong Province are hardworking and can endure hardship, and their wages are very low. The textile mills in Shanghai are in a slump, but the textile mills in Jinan can still make a profit, which is really fortunate.

Lu Province's Financial Revenue and Expenditure Offset 134

The finances of all provinces in the country are causing panic, but Lu Province is an exception. The provincial government's revenue and expenditure are sufficient to offset each other, there is no deficit, the people's burden has not increased, nor has it been seen to increase.

Xiaoqing River Dredging Plan 135

The Yellow River has breached its banks in many places, and Lu Province is greatly alarmed by the potential for the turbulent waters to invade. Regarding the dredging of the Xiaoqing River, Chairman Han's original plan was to ensure that large ships of 600 tons could directly enter a suitable location in the future, and secondly, that ships of 200 tons could directly reach Jinan. In terms of engineering, it is planned to build several dams to equalize the water volume. Lu Province has already spent 700,000 to 800,000 on this, and another 2 million is needed. It is proposed to ask the Economic Commission for assistance. The Economic Commission will refer this to the soon-to-be-established Water Conservancy Commission for discussion and decision.

Qingdao's Construction Has Achieved Considerable Success 136

Mr. Song continued, regarding the construction of Qingdao City, there is much to tell. Everything is more developed than when it was in the hands of the Germans and Japanese. Mayor Shen Honglie is particularly attentive to the lives of the people, building several affordable housing units with rent of only one yuan per month. There are also many emerging public works, among which the establishment of an agricultural improvement agency is particularly effective. All improved varieties of cattle, sheep, pigs, cotton, wheat, etc., are provided free of charge to farmers in the surrounding villages. This kind of work started in Qingdao City. In addition, the government encourages people to grow fruit. However, people are hesitant because of economic difficulties, as it takes five or six years to harvest fruit. However, the city government believes that this is related to international trade and is currently planning to find ways to subsidize it to make people willing to participate.

Informal Discussion of Diplomacy 137

Mr. Song continued, saying that his trip to Qingdao was purely for summer vacation and that his meeting with Ambassador Yan (Huijing) and Minister Gu was accidental and not pre-arranged. After meeting, they talked casually. Of course, diplomacy was also discussed in casual conversation, but there was absolutely no consultation or decision-making. As for suggestions to the government, Ambassador Yan is suffering from heart disease and still needs to go to Peiping to the Xiehe Hospital for diagnosis and treatment, and his return to duty is temporarily undecided. Minister Gu is still staying in Qingdao, and I don't know when he will return to his post. I have not heard about the rumor that Minister Gu is advocating for the conclusion of a non-aggression pact among Pacific countries. Mr. Wang Kemin's visit to Qingdao this time was a normal social courtesy between friends and did not involve any official business.

Loan Negotiations with the Economic Commission are Underway 138

Mr. Song answered reporters' questions, saying that loan applications to the Economic Commission from various parties, such as for the construction of the Qiantang River Railway Bridge, are still under negotiation and no decision has been made. Of course, no contract has been signed yet. I have not yet received a telegram regarding when Dr. Lacis will come to China. The Ministry of Finance and the Ministry of Industry are handling the matter of rescuing the yarn factories operated by Mr. Rong Zongjing, which is not related to the Economic Commission. Although the Economic Commission has a Cotton Industry Control Committee, the work of the Cotton Industry Control Committee is mostly of a permanent nature, and this type of temporary relief is not within its scope.

Mr. Song Denies Forming a Control Committee 139

Silk merchants' leaders such as Chu Fucheng have requested the government to control the silk industry. Matters such as improving silkworm breeds require huge amounts of money. The Economic Commission's financial resources are limited, so it remains to be studied whether it can be done. Mr. Song then denied to reporters the report that the Economic Commission was planning to form a Grain Control Committee, saying that the Economic Commission currently has no such plan. This may be a misunderstanding of the Grain Transportation and Sales Bureau established by the Ministry of Finance. Finally, reporters asked for his opinion on the outflow of silver from our country. Mr. Song replied that it is said that 15 million of our country's silver has flowed out recently, which deserves attention. I will jointly study the advantages and disadvantages with people from the banking sector to determine the advantages and disadvantages.

Travel to Sichuan Delayed, No Plans to Go to Jiangxi 140

Furthermore, he currently has no intention of going to Jiangxi, because there is really no need to meet with Chairman Chiang Kai-shek for the time being. Building Weather Stations and Radio Stations 144

In addition, because the terrain of the line is very high, with many high mountains and ridges along the line, and the climate is harsh, in order to maintain flight safety, the company has prepared 80,000 yuan in cash in addition to ordering special twin-engine aircraft from the United States. Order radio and electrical stations, install radio stations at the Guizhou and Yunnan stations, and set up weather stations at points on the line that impede flight, so as to report weather changes at any time and ensure safety. After the Social Bureau Held Registration

Import of Foreign Rice Gradually Decreases 145

Because Supply and Demand Are Still Appropriate, Market Prices and People's Hearts Are Gradually Stabilized

In order to regulate the people's food and stabilize rice prices, the Municipal Social Bureau has specially stipulated measures for registering the import of foreign rice and instructed rice merchants to implement them. A reporter from Shenshi News Agency learned from the bureau yesterday that this year's drought has caused merchants to purchase foreign rice in droves to speculate and profit. Some of them ordered early and have only now arrived, or they are deliberately transporting them at this time to seek good prices. However, the impact on the national economy is very large, and the excessive import of foreign rice will inevitably lead to a drop in rice prices, which will have a disastrous impact on the harvest of our country's farmers in the future. Since the drought, rice merchants have hoarded rice and waited for higher prices. All the rice of the farmers has fallen into the hands of merchants. If more is imported, the price will inevitably fall back. This matter can be expected to be resolved naturally. The registration of foreign rice is a last resort. If you want to cure the root cause, you must accumulate grain early to prevent hunger. However, although the authorities have seen this, they have not been able to implement it due to limited funds. In the past week, imported foreign rice has either been registered directly with the Social Bureau or forwarded to the Social Bureau by the Rice Industry Association, and taxes have been paid according to law, but the number is extremely small. Recently, the Rice Industry Association claimed that the import of foreign rice has decreased significantly. The reason for this is nothing more than the gradual stabilization of rice prices and the gradual peace of mind of the people. According to the current situation, the import of foreign rice has gradually decreased. If there are no recent changes, the temporarily promulgated measures for the import of foreign rice will be cancelled.

Municipal Industrial Trust Company Holds 163

Guaranteed Fixed Deposits 164

Using Assets of More Than 1.5 Million as Guarantee for Fixed Deposits

The Shanghai Municipal Industrial Trust Company was established by the Shanghai Municipal Government as a municipal business organization. It has been less than a year since its establishment in October of last year, and the progress of its business has been extremely rapid. The company is now holding 1.5 million yuan in guaranteed fixed deposits, using assets of more than 1.5 million yuan as guarantee to seek the safest guarantee for citizens' deposits. This method is still only seen in the operation of trust business. The details are recorded as follows:

The Mission of the Trust Company 165

The company's mission is to focus on handling various trust and transportation businesses, so that citizens can get various benefits. The municipal ferry operated by the company is one proof of this. In addition to handling trust business, other production, insurance, and trust departments also focus on the construction of public utilities, the transfer of urban real estate, and the development of small-capital businesses. The company is willing to do what others are unwilling to do or hesitate to do, and strives to do it for the welfare of the general public.

Guaranteed Fixed Deposits 166

What the company hopes for from the public most is that the public can enjoy the company's services and cooperate closely with the company. After deliberation by the company's board of directors and supervisors, it was decided to hold 1.5 million yuan in guaranteed fixed trust deposits to open a safe investment path for the public. The so-called guarantee refers to the company's assets as a guarantee for deposits, so this deposit is absolutely reliable.

Double Investment Guarantee 167

The company's municipal ferry assets are currently valued at more than 743,000 yuan, and the real estate department's assets are currently valued at more than 773,000 yuan, totaling more than 1.5 million yuan. After inspection and verification by the company's directors, supervisors, and accountants, they are used as a guarantee for this fixed deposit. In addition, after receiving this fixed deposit of 1.5 million yuan, it must be used in the most profitable way to seek the safest guarantee for depositors, which is another layer of guarantee. Therefore, this deposit has an absolute double-layer guarantee.

Proof of Directors and Supervisors 168

The company's directors, such as Xu Xinliu, Wu Yunzhai, Cai Zengji, Li Fuxun, Qin Runqing, Guo Shun, Feng Bingnan, Jin Liren, Shen Yi, Xu Peihuang, Xu Fu, and supervisors such as Lin Kanghou, Yu Hongjun, Wu Zixiang, etc., are all leaders in the financial world, and secretaries and directors of the municipal government. The company's assets are now listed in a table, stamped for certification, and verified and stamped by accountant Xie Lin. Afterwards, all assets will be inspected and advertised by an accountant every six months to show great credibility. Moreover, the proof of the company's directors and supervisors is the same as the fund custody, so the guarantee for depositors is extremely solid. The company also has a "Description of Guaranteed Fixed Trust Deposits," which details the company's assets and the interest rate of fixed deposits in great detail. Citizens who need to read it can send a letter to No. 66 Tianjin Road to the company for collection.

The Municipal Public Utilities Bureau is Proceeding 173

City-Wide Power Plant Interconnection 174

Principles for Mutual Power Supply Established Between Three Companies / Convening Various Power Companies to Standardize Electrical Practices. The power and electricity for the public concessions, Nanshi, and Zhabei areas of this city are supplied by three major power companies: Shanghai Electric Power Company, Zhabei Water and Electricity Company, and China Merchants Electricity Company. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities, recognizing that the electrical business is crucial to the safety of the city and the power source for factories, and that any accident at a power plant would have far-reaching consequences and endless troubles, decided to implement a city-wide power grid unification plan. It convened the aforementioned three companies to discuss interconnection methods. This interconnection cooperation plan is overseen by the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities. If any electrical company experiences a shortage of power supply or an unexpected accident, other companies can immediately provide power, preventing adverse effects such as power outages. This plan requires the special adjustment of one generator and two large cables connecting the three electrical companies. The Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities has drafted the principles regarding expenses and other procedures and is currently actively consulting with all relevant parties to complete the city-wide power grid unification plan as soon as possible. Two Announcements from the Jianghai Customs 178

Measures for Ships Not Carrying Cargo Passing Through Foreign Ports / Auction of Confiscated Injection Needles and Syringes Scheduled. Berleth, Commissioner of Customs of the Jianghai Customs, issued two announcements yesterday, regarding the prohibition of ships traveling between trading ports without carrying cargo from passing through foreign ports without declaring to customs, and the scheduled auction of injection needles. The announcements are copied below for the attention of shipowners and the public.

Announcement One 179

Regarding the transportation of domestic goods from one trading port to another through foreign ports, specific regulations have been established for compliance. The following are the important points to be noted: For ships traveling from one trading port to another without carrying cargo, if the name of the foreign port to be passed through is not declared to the exporting customs when the ship clears customs, it is not allowed to pass through the foreign port under the pretext of adding coal or other reasons. Those who dare to violate this rule will be fined up to 500 national currency. All shipowners, agents, and captains of ships must take note of this announcement.

Announcement Two 180

This Customs currently has confiscated injection needles, syringes, and other items for auction. Those who hold a license from the Shanghai Municipal Health Bureau are allowed to bring their licenses to the Transportation Department of this Customs between 2:00 PM and 4:00 PM on the 21st and 22nd of this month to inspect and submit bids. The bids will be opened at 10:00 AM on the 24th of this month. This is a special announcement. Wu Ting Sheng Goes North

Guiding Farmers in Curing Tobacco Leaves 181

Optimistic Prospects for Controlled Production. Since the establishment of the American Tobacco Leaf Improvement Committee in Shanghai, it has sent personnel to Xuchang, Yuxian, Jiaxian, Xiangcheng, and other counties to inspect the lives of local farmers, collect statistics on local production, and test the quality of the products. According to the survey, Jiaxian has the highest production and the best quality. It is reported that the committee has formulated tens of thousands of copies of "Guidelines for American Tobacco Leaves" because the time for curing new leaves is approaching. The guidelines detail the various procedures for transplanting, cultivation, harvesting, and kiln dimensions and will be distributed to farmers. The committee has also requested its executive committee member Mr. Wu Ting Sheng to personally provide guidance. Mr. Wu took the night train to Beijing last night and will transfer to the north. According to Mr. Wu, the mission is not only to improve tobacco leaves but also to improve tobacco seeds. The first step is to prohibit farmers from saving seeds. All tobacco seeds will be distributed by the committee free of charge. In the long run, this will prevent self-destruction. Then, the committee will distribute seeds according to the annual needs, preventing overproduction and harm to both parties. The future is very optimistic.

Major Crimes 186

The original announcement is as follows (omitted above). I secretly believe that crises are lurking everywhere, robbery is imminent, the Divine Land is sinking, and the waiting is palpable. The teachings of Buddhism advocate equality for all beings, and their aspiration is vast, just as the Confucian pursuit of the ultimate good has the sentiment of being overly cautious. Therefore, this association adheres to these true principles and strives to put them into practice. It seeks to protect the safety of animals and eliminate the evil thoughts of human slaughter, which may avert crises and eliminate robbery.

Moreover, governments of various countries have enacted laws and regulations to protect animals, which are numerous. Even the ancient sages and worthies of our country, such as Tang of Shang opening the nets and Yiyin keeping away from the kitchen, were praised as the ultimate virtues by later generations. We should learn from Tang and Confucius and follow the example of the great powers. We should urgently provide a secure and positive guarantee for the lives and treatment of our helpless companions who coexist in the universe, so as not to fail in our heavenly duty of protecting life. For example, the dogs raised in various places are also one of our companions. How can we ignore their lives and treatment? Recently, municipal authorities in Jiangsu and Zhejiang have been concerned about rectifying the appearance of cities and the indiscriminate breeding of dogs. All ownerless stray dogs, regardless of whether they have rabies or other diseases, are arrested and subjected to cruel treatments such as strangulation or caustic injection. For example, Shen Bao reported on July 12 that Chairman Han of Jinan shot more than 2,000 stray dogs, which is shocking. This association has repeatedly tried to dissuade them, but they all claimed that there was nowhere to place them and that the words were empty. As the saying goes, preparation leads to success, and the fault lies in our failure to plan ahead. This association aims to implement its advocacy of animal protection, considering all aspects, and has thus made a motion to appeal to monasteries in various places to jointly provide relief. We humbly request all elders of the mountains to widely implement boundless benevolence and compassion, following the example of raising livestock, fish, and turtles, and to provide free separate feeding with surplus food so that innocent stray dogs can live out their natural lives and realize the fulfillment of equality for all beings. We previously drafted the method for raising stray dogs, and we are fortunate to have your understanding and generosity. It is truly magnificent. China Animal Protection Association Tax Collection Agencies

Measures for Investigating and Detaining Tax-Evading Goods 193

The Two Roads Bureau issued an order to the Transportation Department and the Police Department, stating: "The Ministry of Railways issued Order No. 10592, and the Ministry of Finance issued Letter No. 4579, which stated that in the future, if merchants privately transport tax-evading goods and the tax collection agency discovers and has concrete evidence and applies in advance for detention, the Railway Bureau should immediately instruct the station warehouse to notify the applying agency to send personnel to the station to witness the release of the goods when the merchant picks them up. However, the inspection of the goods should still be carried out outside the station. Please notify all roads to comply with this order, so as to avoid requesting to enter the station or board the train for inspection." In addition to distribution, this order also urgently instructs the department to comply with it.

Meeting at the Hong Residence 201

At the appointed time, I went to wait for ten minutes. Mr. Yang and his grandson arrived, and Chen Zhujun also came to the living room. I saw that Binghu's face looked ashen, and I was quite worried. Binghu spoke first, saying, "I am very sorry for this matter." I immediately comforted him. After everyone had spoken, Binghu suddenly wanted to have a private talk with Chen. Chen refused again and again, but finally agreed to go into the bathroom with Binghu. After a moment, I faintly heard three or four thuds. Hong Chengde went to the bathroom to check and saw that both of them had died tragically. We then briefly looked around and reported to the police station, which sent Western Detective Watson to investigate. They found a handgun and a suicide note in the bathroom. The envelope said, "To be buried together." The letter was addressed to his grandfather. Later, the court examined the bodies. Because it had nothing to do with me, I did not go to the autopsy. Later, I heard that Chen Wangshi confessed at the time,

"I Was Killed" 202

The court had to order me to appear in court. The next day, I immediately obeyed the summons and confessed everything. The woman replied, "Because I had no money and was all alone, I had to ask friends and relatives for help, so I have been delayed until now." Then, He Yunpu, the detective from the Jing'an Police Station who handled the case, reported the situation of the investigation at the Hong's residence on the day he went with Western Detective Watson. He said that the bodies of the man and woman were lying in the bathroom, separated only by a chamber pot. The pistol and the letter were found at the entrance of the room. However, according to Xu Hongjun, the doorman there, on April 26, Mr. and Mrs. Hong, together with three other people, brought the deceased Chen Zhujun here and used those three people to monitor the woman's actions. On the 28th, the woman tried to escape but was stopped by the Hong family's maid. Chen Hengcai Was Executed by Hanging Yesterday 203

Chen's last words were for his wife to remarry and leave the daughter. Before the execution, he sang Peking Opera loudly. Mr. Zhang, a former Qing dynasty county magistrate from Huzhou, had been dead for many years. He had two wives, both named Su, who lived at 762 Carter Road. Yesterday morning, the police took Chen from the prison and sent him to the Third Criminal Court for execution. Judge Shen Shanzeng asked him if he had any last words or letters to his family. Chen was short in stature and calm in demeanor. He said that he had a wife and a daughter at home. If his wife wanted to remarry, he asked his sisters to keep the daughter. Then, together with the entire case file and photographs, he was escorted by car to the Second Prison execution ground in Caohejing. According to the law, he was hanged for his crime. Two Gangs of Butchers Fought 204

The gangs from Pudong and Jiangyin have a deep-seated feud. The slaughterhouse company established by the French Municipal Council on Min Ti Ni Yin Road in the French Concession, commonly known as the half-slaughter company, employs butchers and workers who are divided into gangs from Pudong and Jiangyin, each with its own leaders. However, due to their duties, the workers from the two gangs have repeatedly had undercurrents and disputes. On the 26th of last month, butchers from the Pudong gang went to Nanjing to buy live pigs and had a fight with the Jiangyin gang, injuring three butchers from the Pudong gang. The case was reported to the Public Security Bureau, which arrested two members of the Jiangyin gang, who were transferred to the Local Court for trial and sentenced to a fine of 40 yuan each. Seven fleeing suspects were also ordered to be arrested. Because of this, the workers from the two gangs harbored even deeper resentment and constantly thought of revenge. Recently, the situation became urgent. The Chinese and Western directors of the slaughterhouse company, fearing a major disaster, went to the Songshan Road Police Station on the 16th to report the incident and request the dispatch of detectives to protect the area around the company to ensure safety. Unexpectedly, at 11:30 PM that evening, a group of butchers from the Jiangyin gang entered the company from Glock Road to start their slaughtering work. When they arrived near Wenyuanfang at the north end of the company's back door, they were suddenly attacked by a group of butchers from the Pudong gang who rushed out of Wenyuanfang Lane, blocking the Jiangyin gang from entering the company. During the argument, a fight broke out. The Pudong gang butchers, each armed with knives and axes, wildly stabbed and slashed at the Jiangyin gang butchers. At that time, Xu Zhongqiu (23 years old), Xu Mingde (22 years old), Jiang Fuda (23 years old), and Ren Jinbao (23 years old), all from the Jiangyin gang living at No. 11 Wenyuanfang, and Yao Shengxiang (28 years old), from the Jiangyin gang living at No. 5 Bao'anfang, were injured by axes and knives, bleeding profusely. For a time, the noise was deafening, and the sirens of the police cars sounded, as if facing a major enemy. Chinese police officers from No. 505 and No. 621 arrived and arrested Qin Haichang (also known as A Xiang, 23 years old, from Jiading), Gao Shanyun (26 years old, from Chuansha), and Wang Ren'er (24 years old, from Haimen), three members of the Pudong gang living at No. 9 Huabao Fang on Lagenna Road, and took them to the police station. At the same time, the injured were sent to Guangci Hospital. After examination by doctors, Xu Zhongqiu had a head wound, and Xu Mingde and Yao Shengxiang were stabbed in the buttocks. Since the injuries were minor, they were bandaged and discharged from the hospital to return home. Jiang Fuda and Ren Jinbao were cut several times by knives and axes and were more seriously injured and hospitalized for treatment. At noon yesterday, the police sent the defendants to the First Criminal Court of the Second Special District, where Judge Zhang Chaozuo interrogated them. Yuan Jiahan, the police lawyer, stated the case, saying that the defendants were detained for crimes such as assault and restriction of freedom, and the police needed to conduct a detailed investigation and requested a postponement. The defendants were temporarily detained pending further investigation. Then, the victims Xu Zhongqiu, Xu Mingde, and Yao Shengxiang testified that when they were going to work at the company, the defendants and dozens of others came out to stop them, not allowing them to enter the company. Their boss, Chen Jinhai, held a gun to intimidate them and ordered the defendants to commit violence, resulting in them being injured by knives and axes. They requested an investigation. When questioned, the defendants denied committing the violence and hired lawyer Wang Shizong to defend them. The court ordered the hearing to be adjourned to the 22nd and the defendants were returned to custody. The victims were ordered to submit to a medical examination at the forensic office to verify their injuries. A tragic event in the world.

Good News and Bad News 205

Fu Yuechun, how pitiful! Drowned on the day of his engagement. Fu Yuechun, a Ningbo native residing at No. 6 Xinlong Lane, Xianji Road, Nanshi, was only 20 years old. He was a deputy steward on the Taikoo Company's Ninghai ship. He had just resigned a week ago and was unemployed at home. His father was a deputy steward on the company's Daming ship. Yesterday was the date of Yuechun's engagement. The Ninghai ship had arrived in port the day before, so his father came home yesterday to help take care of things and distribute large amounts of fruit and steamed buns to relatives and friends according to Ningbo customs. He instructed Yuechun to handle the ship's affairs for one day. At 3:45 PM, Yuechun bought some Western pastries from Puxi and took the Taikoo express ferry back to the ship at the Yangjingbang Wharf. When the ferry arrived at the Huatong Wharf in Pudong, Yuechun, eager to disembark, accidentally slipped from the wharf and fell into the river, immediately sinking without a trace. He tragically drowned. When colleagues on the ship learned of this, they sent a message to Yuechun's home. Just as relatives and friends were gathered together, warmly celebrating, they suddenly heard the bad news. It was like a bolt from the blue, and the whole family was inconsolable. The family reported the news to the bride's family and asked a friend to report to the Customs Water Police Station to request the retrieval of the body. Chinese Detective Gu Wenkui investigated the scene and hired people to search for the body. By evening, the body had not been found. It was truly tragic.

Frustrated Compatriot Comes to Shanghai for Food, Commits Suicide 219

Teng Tao Swallows Opium and Kills Herself: Teng Tao, an Anhui woman, was forty-seven years old. Her husband, Teng Wenyu, both worked in the Shenxin No. 7 Cotton Mill on Jinsheng Road. They lived in the factory's dormitory. Teng had a younger brother who lived in their hometown, working as a farmer. He had four children. Recently, due to poor farming conditions and a difficult life, he intended to send two of his sons to Shanghai to ask his brother to take care of them, hoping to make a living. He immediately wrote a letter to his brother, detailing the hardships in the countryside and requesting his consent. After receiving the letter, Teng, out of brotherly affection, felt obliged to help and immediately replied, agreeing to the request. However, the matter was discovered by his wife the day before yesterday. Because she did not get along well with her uncle, she argued with her husband upon hearing about it. It was too late to change anything, and she was extremely frustrated. She suddenly had the thought of ending her life and secretly swallowed opium to commit suicide. When Teng discovered her, she was groaning in bed. He rushed her to Tongren Hospital, and then transferred her to Guangren Hospital for treatment, but it was ineffective. She died around 4 PM that day. The hospital reported it to the Yulin Road Police Station, which ordered detectives to investigate. The body was then taken to the autopsy room on Feilun Road. Yesterday morning, Guo Wei, a prosecutor from the First Special District Local Court, was dispatched to the scene to examine the body. After questioning Teng Wenyu, the deceased's husband, who recounted the previous events, Prosecutor Guo declared that the deceased, Teng Tao, a female, had indeed died from opium poisoning. The body was released to her husband, Teng Wenyu, to arrange for burial.

Hydrographic Office Notice of Sailing Vessels 220

Notice No. 108 from the Hydrographic Office of the Navy Department Regarding Obstacles to Navigation. Regarding floating obstacles hazardous to navigation (Changes will be announced further): (1) Location: East Coast of the Republic of China; Date of Discovery: August 8th of this year; Location: Approximately 119 degrees 47 minutes East Longitude, 26 degrees 6 minutes North Latitude; Description: An overturned civilian vessel. (2) Location: East Coast of the Republic of China; Date of Discovery: August 11th of this year; Location: Approximately 122 degrees 10 minutes East Longitude, 29 degrees 0 minutes North Latitude; Description: A drifting civilian vessel. (Note) The directions given in this navigation notice are calculated from 0 degrees True North, turning clockwise to 359 degrees. The direction of the lights is calculated from the sea, considering the distance of the light force in clear weather. Fog signals are only used in foggy weather, and further explanations will be given when necessary. The depth records are calculated according to the reference plane used in the largest scale chart.

The Chicken and Egg Problem 229

– Reply to Mr. Wang Zaifu – The question of whether the chicken or the egg came first is not limited to chickens; it is a question of the origin of all living things. The real essence of this question is: were all living things initially already living things, or were they initially only in egg form? To solve this problem, knowledge of biology is essential, and a correct way of thinking is also necessary. If we only have scattered scientific knowledge without a correct method to systematize it, we will still not be able to understand this problem consistently. In the past scientific community, there were two solutions to the problem of the origin of life. The first is the so-called spontaneous generation theory, which believes that all living things arise spontaneously from non-living matter. According to this theory, the chicken was initially a chicken and did not necessarily come from an egg, just as rice turns into mice and rotten grass turns into fireflies. This theory was refuted in the second half of the nineteenth century by the German microbiologist Pasteur. Last year, Dr. Luo Guangting of China claimed to have confirmed this theory again, but scholars across the country exposed his absurdity. Now we all know that this theory is untenable. The second theory is that life absolutely cannot arise spontaneously. The reason there is life on Earth is that there were originally seeds of life in the universe, and these seeds were brought to Earth by fragments of celestial bodies such as meteorites and gradually developed into their current form. According to this theory, life was initially in the form of (eggs), and only when it encountered a suitable environment on Earth did it hatch into living things. This theory does not completely solve the problem. It assumes that life originates from seeds, but if we ask how the seeds were formed, there is no way to answer. Because this theory is completely opposed to the theory of spontaneous generation, it does not admit that seeds can arise from non-living matter. If they did not arise from non-living matter, then where did they come from? In the end, it seems we can only use God's creation to explain it, leading us into the realm of religious souls! Currently, we all know that living things are constantly evolving. During the process of evolution, the structure of living things changes from simple to complex, from lower to higher. In other words, the more ancient the living things, the simpler their body structure. Thirty million years ago, the world only had large reptiles, which were much lower in the scale of evolution than modern humans, cattle, horses, tigers, and leopards. However, tens of millions of years before that thirty million years ago, there was an era when there were not even reptiles. At that time, there were only simple animals such as coelenterates and shellfish. However, these simple animals were still much more complex than the even more ancient creatures. The more ancient and simpler creatures were single-celled organisms. No matter how simple coelenterates and the like are, they are always composed of tens of thousands of cells. A single-celled organism can form an independent organism with just one cell. Many species of these single-celled organisms still remain today, continuing their humble lives in the microscopic world. The theory of evolution has obtained definitive and irrefutable evidence from paleontology, serology, comparative anatomy, and other aspects. Now, no one can overturn it anymore. We are now certain that the various races of living things do not arise spontaneously from non-living matter, but develop and differentiate along a long evolutionary journey. If races could be directly produced from non-living matter, it would fundamentally shake the laws of evolution. Since we cannot deny the laws of evolution, the Luo-style theory of spontaneous generation, such as rice turning into mice, cannot stand. But at the same time, because we believe that the most ancient living things are the simplest single-celled organisms, we cannot deny that at some point in the distant past, the living things of that time must have been so simple that they were almost indistinguishable from non-living matter. Furthermore, we can even assume that in a certain primitive period, non-living matter formed the first living things through certain chemical and physical actions. These living things were the beginning of all later living things, a small life so simple that it was almost indistinguishable from non-living matter. This is also a kind of spontaneous generation theory, but this spontaneous generation theory is absolutely different from the theory of rice turning into mice and has a scientific basis in evolutionary theory. This spontaneous generation theory is precisely the conclusion that the theory of evolution must inevitably reach. According to the results of today's scientific research, the form of the first living things that we can assume must still be the form of single-celled organisms, but the first single-celled organisms must have been much simpler than the single-celled organisms that remain today. If we say that the form of a single cell is the form of an egg, and that all living things in the world evolved from single-celled organisms, then we can immediately reach the conclusion that it was (the egg that came before the chicken, not the chicken before the egg). But things cannot be said so simply. We must pay attention to the fact that the chicken is a multicellular animal, and the reproductive life of multicellular organisms is different from that of single cells. The hundreds of millions of cells that make up the entire body of the chicken will eventually die along with the chicken itself, so it must use the method of laying eggs to maintain the existence of the race. But for single-celled organisms, they can not only survive on their own but also reproduce by dividing themselves. Therefore, in single-celled organisms, there is no distinction between (chicken) and (egg). The single cell itself is the chicken and also the egg. The two opposing functions of (chicken) and (egg) are fused together in single-celled organisms, a hidden contradiction, a potential action. At this time, we simply cannot ask whether the egg came before the chicken or the chicken before the egg. We can also say that the egg came before the egg, or the chicken came before the chicken. Because you cannot strictly say whether a single-celled animal itself is an egg or a chicken. Therefore, the question of whether the chicken or the egg came first can only arise after there is a chicken. In other words, this question only has meaning for multicellular animals. The phenomenon of laying eggs and eggs hatching from eggs is a unique phenomenon in multicellular organisms. If there were no multicellular organisms in living things, there would never be such a phenomenon. Thus, we know that the establishment of multicellular organisms is a prerequisite for this phenomenon, which also means that the establishment of the chicken itself is a prerequisite for laying eggs. Based on this point, we should regard the chicken as the foundation and say that the chicken came before the egg, not the egg before the chicken. From the example of biological evolution, the simplest multicellular organisms do not use the phenomenon of producing seeds to carry out their reproductive functions. The daughter bodies of Volvox separate directly from the mother body, and coelenterates such as Hydra reproduce by budding. This tells us that in the process of biological evolution, when multicellular organisms were first formed, they did not immediately have the phenomenon of producing seeds. The phenomenon of producing seeds only appeared when multicellular organisms had developed to a more complex and advanced state. At such times, the opposing functions of the chicken and the egg differentiated from a latent state to a manifest state, and the cycle of chicken laying egg and egg hatching chicken began. In this way, we can conclude that in the beginning, the egg was laid by the chicken. Afterwards, the chicken and the egg infinitely cycle each other as cause and effect. We acknowledge the cyclical action and mutual interaction. But we also need to find the ultimate starting point in the cycle and the fundamental guiding role in the interaction. Otherwise, we will become eclecticists.

Free Talk

Trends 230

— Bo

Some say that the evolution of the times is a straight line, others say it is like ripples, and still others have determined that it is a cycle based on the fact that the size of cuffs gets bigger and smaller, and then smaller and bigger. These are all profound theories, but the people who say these things have forgotten one thing: they have forgotten that the times are determined by human beings. They think that this is something that concerns another planet, but they do not know that it concerns themselves and their kind.

How do you decide the times? If you are sitting in a study reciting poetry or listening to cicadas chirping in the shade of a tree, the further you are from society, the less impact you have. However, when you step onto the political stage, or have a large deposit in the bank, or have the talent of a silver tongue, you vaguely feel that you have the power to manipulate the times. At that time, you will say (bullshit, bullshit, this is really outrageous)!

But what if you have a feeling? You must have ideals, you must have management skills, you must have actions, and you must have effects. Then, are the times affected? Here is a very simple example that can prove it:

In public amusement places, there is often a small cage, and in the cage there is often a pair of wire balls, like the meridians on a geography textbook, in which several white mice are kept, stepping on this cage day and night, going up! Forward! - But the distance does not decrease, and this kind of management is quite painstaking. The distance traveled in a day should be several miles. This has become one of the entertainments for the audience, interesting!

Suppose we think for the mice, instead of driving a car in a cage, run out and run around. At least the distance can be different, right? The outside is not as comfortable as in the cage, but it is also surrounded by narrowness and is not ridiculed by the audience. Where do you want to run so hard? To make people happy forever?

It is really what they say (the wisdom and foolishness of people are like mouse droppings)! The same amount of power is used, but the results are very different; everyone has the power to decide the times, as long as they break the surrounding cage.

(Literature Dies, Disaster Won’t Stop) 231

– Huang Pingling

In a letter to the mass language expert Cao Juren, Mr. Wu Zhihui expressed his extreme aversion to literature in the Free Talk section of Shen Bao. He wrote down two famous words of hatred: (Literature dies, disaster won’t stop.) We are not surprised that Mr. Wu wrote these two angry words, because Mr. Wu has always been dedicated to promoting science and engineering.

However, Mr. Wu was not the first to advocate science and engineering. From Zhang Zhidong's advocacy of Western learning for application and Chinese learning as the foundation, to the era of Westernization self-strengthening theory in the late Qing Dynasty, to the heyday of vocational education in the fifth and sixth years of the Republic of China, to the current era of focusing on science and engineering, it can be seen that China has been promoting science and technology and advocating craftsmanship at all times. The Chinese students who were sent to study abroad as early as the Daoguang era, which is now sixty years ago. Among them, about seven-tenths of the students sent abroad studied science and engineering, and three-tenths studied military affairs. As for the country officially sending young people to study literature abroad, there has simply never been such a thing (except for those who pay their own expenses). It can be said that literature has never been promoted in China.

Mr. Wu suspects that China's science and engineering are inferior to others because of the large number of people studying literature. In fact, this is not the case at all. According to our experience in running literary and artistic publications for six or seven years, we feel that at this moment, we cannot find even a dozen people in the country who can write decent works. There are only two or three literary and artistic publications in the country that are relatively decent. Almost everyone feels the lack of creation in these two or three publications. Recently, none of the three or two film companies in China are not short of scripts. If things continue like this, Chinese literature will definitely die; however, after literature dies, whether the disaster can be stopped is the responsibility of those who study science and engineering.

Science and engineering has been promoted for sixty years, and the country has spent no less than tens of millions of trillions of gold pounds on tuition fees. Now, our daily necessities, in addition to the application of imported goods, are only devolved to the stone age of barrenness. Whose fault is it? China, which has been known as an agricultural country for four thousand years, still uses the old tricks invented by our ancestors. Whose fault is it? Those who study commerce, those who study engineering, those who study architecture... are abundant in China, but to this day, they cannot imitate an electric light bulb or make a screw by themselves. No matter how big or small the civil engineering projects are, they all rely on foreigners to be our consultants. Whose fault is it?

(Literature) cannot be used as clothing in the cold, nor can it be used as food when hungry. It is indeed useless waste. However, everyone attributes the brilliant achievements of European and American science and culture today to the Renaissance of the seventeenth century. I don't know why. Even the militarist Hitler could not help but respect the old writer Hauptmann as much as possible and spend huge sums of money to build Wagner's music memorial hall and hold a grand centenary memorial for Goethe. I don't know why. The heroic Mussolini treated the intellectuals in the country with great courtesy, especially the literary writer D'Annunzio. I don't know why. France held a state funeral only five times, and the literary artists Hugo and France occupied two of them. I don't know why. Recently, those in power in Soviet Russia are mostly from the literary world, but it does not hinder their five-year plan. It is a fact; the literary atmosphere in Japan is already so strong, and the Ministry of Education still assists the progress of literature and art. The University of Tokyo has not abolished the Department of Literature, which is also a fact. No one in China has openly promoted literary and artistic movements, and the country has never sacrificed a tuition fee for literature. The government has never had any plans for literary and artistic facilities. It is only with the interest of a very few people that they occasionally make minimal contributions to literature, and they cannot avoid being cursed so viciously by Mr. Wu Zhihui. It is so pitiful.

Of course, Mr. Wu is eagerly looking forward to China's road to revival, but if there are no literary and artistic figures working diligently to improve the people's will to move upward, change the people's increasingly declining morbidity, and invigorate the nation's great spirit, I am afraid that although there are many people studying science and engineering, and there are many people promoting science and engineering, it always feels a little difficult to make the country receive the practical effects of science and engineering! Because although they are studying science and engineering, they are still holding on to the old idea of (studying well and then becoming an official). No such fool will really run to the scientific and engineering fields.

The Problem of (Showing the Goods) 232

— Fulan

The discussion of the mass language problem has been going on until now, and some people still think that mass language literature is a brand new, sensational thing, which is really not right. For example, Mr. So-and-so's article (Try it out) has this meaning.

Establishing mass language literature does not completely (negate) vernacular Chinese and (create) a new mass language writing with three heads and six arms. It is precisely to remove the harmful elements from vernacular Chinese - the mixed classical Chinese, Europeanized tone, and everything that does not suit the needs of the masses. Although mass language writing is different from vernacular Chinese, it does not completely negate the vernacular Chinese since the May Fourth Movement and come up with a completely (new) writing. We know that the growth and reform of language and writing are slow, and there must be a process of reform and change in it. A completely new mass language writing cannot (suddenly) be produced. If it can, it is not mass language writing, but (heavenly scripture)!

Many people have this (high-profile) tendency, and then two questions arise: (Show the goods) and (What form should mass language writing take).

Mr. So-and-so also said: (Take out the mass language works, take out the model of mass language writing) (The word 'model' can be replaced by the word '樣式'). This attitude of urgently wanting people to take out the goods is not very reasonable. Mass language literature is not (red bean shaved ice). You only need to shave the ice, add red bean soup, and you can immediately send it to your mouth. The promotion of mass language writing is to make people first aware of this need, and then gradually reform and complete it in this direction - apply the new popular spoken language of the masses, remove the mixed classical Chinese and Europeanized tone, and grow together in the development of the public's life. The goods are there, but they are not like red bean shaved ice that can immediately quench your thirst. If you want to see the goods and bargain now, then you can only laugh like a mass language work (made) by someone. It can be said that this has not touched the establishment of the mass language literature problem itself!

Because of the urgent need for (goods), some people advocate the implementation of local dialects under the question of (what form should mass language literature take). Therefore, they advocate writing in local dialects, thinking that it is a mass language literature good. This is a consistent mistake. I once published two articles on the opinions of local dialects in the supplement of Hua Ri Bao. My meaning is that it is not bad to use local dialects naturally. If you take local dialects as an important factor of mass language, forcibly use them together, or completely write in local dialects, it is impossible in any case. There are many people who have raised this issue for discussion, both in favor and against. However, I still firmly advocate that pure local dialects are not important for the establishment of mass language writing, and I think that those who propose pure local dialect literature are somewhat making the mistake of being eager to show the goods to others.

One Year of Unemployment 233

— Shen Shengshi

Since leaving school last summer vacation, the issue of finding a way out has been bothering me. I asked friends and relatives to write letters of introduction and ran around looking for opportunities, but I was completely disappointed. I had no money to dream of going abroad with friends, and I couldn't find a position. In fact, I didn't have too many extravagant hopes. I would be willing to take even a small clerk's position, but even such a wish could not be fulfilled, so I started to live as a recluse in my hometown.

The seasons quickly turned around. After the scorching summer, there was a windy and rainy autumn; watching the snowflakes fly in front of the court, after the New Year, it was the good weather of the new spring. I watched the peach blossoms bloom and fall in loneliness, and the rich spring also slowly stepped through the world. In the blink of an eye, it was another hot day. Now it is the time of year when I lost my job last year! But I am still stuck in my hometown, unable to find a place to eat, staring at the sunlight in front of the window, moving down the wall in the morning and quietly moving back in the evening, living day by day, and the poor life is pressing down on me, as if there is nothing to say—

—Unemployment has been a year!

Staring at the calendar on the wall that has been torn off for most of the year, I sighed so much.

My unemployment was actually expected. Living in today's era, especially in this year of social depression, it is very appropriate and inevitable that someone like me is listed among the unemployed. The worldwide economic depression has certainly affected the livelihood of an unknown small person; on the one hand, my own excessive uselessness cannot cater to a rogue-style society. I am always foolishly trying to retain a little honesty in being a human being, so I am more likely to be frustrated and fail.

In the vast world, I can't find a place to eat, and I am stuck in a narrow cage-like hometown, like a parasite, sucking the dried-up intestinal walls of my grandmother and father, who have no fat. A wounded heart is gradually sinking towards dusk and will form a hysterical patient.

It's the time of year when the summer is over and the autumn is beginning again. Unemployment has been a year!

Last year, today, I was wandering on the street. This year, I am still wandering in the same way. A wounded heart is screaming:

—I want to live—!

Singing Doesn’t Stop, Pulling Doesn’t Break for the Sake of Living 234

—

Women and Dogs 235

— Pu Feng

No matter where you go, to Singapore, Java, or Hong Kong, it is most common to see Western women walking down the street with a dog in their hands; even in Shanghai, we can easily get proof.

Why are dogs so especially loved by women?

They can guard the door, they specialize in bullying beggars dressed in rags, and they are loyal to their masters. This is what we know about dogs. However, now, the Pekingese dogs being held in their hands are not used for guarding the door, but rather for being loyal to their masters, playing with them day and night. In a word, they are just a kind of toy for the master.

If women need toys, just as children need candy, dogs, this thing obviously has enough qualifications to be loved by women!

When you walk on Avenue Joffre, whether you see dogs being held by Western women or see them being carried in cars, and noble women are caressing them tenderly, you don't need to envy them. The problem is that they are indeed a kind of toy. - Unemployment, hunger, and cold should make us angry that they feed beef to dogs every day and feel ashamed to be human. Are you still drooling over them?

Naturally, they have truly become a kind of toy. If God is always speaking fairly for the rich, then dogs, they should enjoy happiness. Dogs, precisely because they are being raised, feel happy, and they are proudly thinking that this happiness will continue endlessly!

But can you say that Pekingese dogs are the only ones being held in women's arms and held in women's hands? I believe that without a prophet to testify for us, many men are being raised like Pekingese dogs; similarly, their dreams will never wake up!

Old Man (7) 236

— Jin Yi

But now, he thought, shaking his head.

It was not early, and the shop opposite had been closed for half an hour. He had no choice but to stand up and walk forward two steps, staggering, but suddenly, someone broke in.

(Who is it?) he thought in his heart. His eyes were really a little blurry. If it was just because he was old, his strength was a little useless. That's not the whole story; it was more because he drank a little more wine that he couldn't see anything clearly.

He wiped his eyes with his palm, and the person who came in shouted in a loud voice:

(You're really old, old man, can't you recognize me?)

(Followed by a burst of rude laughter, the person's face moved closer to him.)

He could see some of it now. It was a face like a large, fat pumpkin, with a beard that connected to his sideburns and hair, but his nose was like a hanging red pepper. He remembered, he called out:

(Alise, is that you? You haven't been here for a month.)

He was happy, as if he had drunk more wine, and spoke in a short voice, deliberately shaking his hand and patting the person's shoulder.

(Wasn't I here two weeks ago? Your memory is really a little bad.)

(The memory isn't bad, it must be————) he said, paused, shaking his head, (it must be because I drank a little more wine.)

After saying that, he raised his eyelids to look at the person, but the person was staring at the fancy hat he had bought years ago, paying no attention to his words at all.

He deliberately tilted his body and bumped into the person, repeating the sentence:

(Yesterday, I drank a little more wine!)

(Ah, old man, no wonder you're so drunk. It would be a little troublesome if you fell down!)

Educational News

Severe Drought in Zhejiang

Sharp Decline in New Student Enrollment at Various Schools 237

In recent years, our country's rural economy has collapsed, financial instability has caused panic, and this year we have suffered another drought, greatly affecting the autumn harvest. In the past, even families with a hundred acres of land could barely afford the expenses of a middle school student. It is now known that the summer vacation for all levels of schools in Zhejiang Province is about to end. For the 23rd academic year, the enrollment of new students has been completed in some schools, and those that have not yet been held will begin their entrance exams in the next few days. Taking Hangzhou City as an example, the number of applicants for the entrance examinations for junior high schools and above has decreased unprecedentedly this year, especially in private middle schools with shorter histories and higher tuition fees. Even schools like the Provincial Hangzhou High School, Provincial Hangzhou Junior High School, Municipal Middle School, and Hangzhou Normal School, which used to attract around a thousand applicants each year, have seen a sharp decline of four to five hundred applicants, despite the Education Department's efforts to implement scholarships, grants, and reduced meal fees for normal school students in these difficult times to help impoverished students. However, the National Zhejiang University has seen an increase in applicants due to its lower tuition fees. As for the Central Aviation School in Jianqiao, Hangzhou, which offers tuition and board free of charge, the number of applicants has increased even more. This clearly shows that the social and economic panic has reached an extreme. Northeastern Youth.

Recent News from the Relief and Education Office 238

▲Funding for Student Relief is Being Distributed: Several recent news items from the Northeastern Youth Education Relief Office of the Ministry of Education are excerpted below: (1) The relief fund for Northeastern students, recently amounting to 40,000 yuan, has been received by the Relief Office and is now being remitted to various schools in provinces and cities that have Northeastern youths to be forwarded to the students. (Currently, Northeastern students are present in more than a dozen provinces and cities, such as Beijing, Shanghai, Hangzhou, Tianjin, Wuhan, Guangzhou, Qingdao, Shandong, and others, with the most students in Beijing and Tianjin.) Approximately 4,000 Northeastern students in various provinces and cities have requested assistance, and after investigation and verification, over 3,000 have been deemed eligible. The subsidy methods are as follows: For university students, the general expense (meal fee) is 4 yuan per person per month, and the special expense (for books, etc., only for excellent students) is 5 yuan per person per month, calculated over five months per semester. Excellent students can receive 45 yuan in both general and special expenses per semester, while ordinary students receive only the general expense of 20 yuan per semester. For high school students, the general (meal fee) expense is 3.5 yuan per person per month, and the special expense (for books, etc.) is 4 yuan. Excellent students can receive 37.5 yuan in both general and special expenses per semester. For junior high school students, the general expense is 3.5 yuan per person, and the special expense is 3 yuan. Excellent students can receive 32.5 yuan per semester. The subsidy for primary school students is only 3 yuan per semester for tuition fees. (2) Zhongshan Middle School in North China was established with high school, junior high school, junior vocational, and supplementary classes, with a total of 800 students. This term, after the summer vacation, the school is enrolling (applications are currently being accepted, and the examination will be held in the twenties of this month) senior vocational students and high school students in the third grade, as well as junior high school students and students for supplementary classes, totaling about 200 students. In addition, 200 students from the privately run Zhixing Middle School (which specializes in accepting Northeastern students and recently merged into Zhongshan Middle School) will also be added. After the summer vacation, Zhongshan Middle School will have 1,200 students. (3) The Relief Office plans to hold examinations for Northeastern students to study abroad in the early part of this month after the spring and autumn seasons.

Children's Health Camp (II) 255

Zhou Shangxian ▲Social Activity Education: Hosted by me. During this summer vacation, I spent almost all my time living in the camp, carefully planning activities. There were also two guidance directors, Tu Yunqin and Huang Qionghe, and nine counselors, Chen Caiying, Li Jiefang, Zhang Dede, Ma Ji, Luo Meixue, Xu Zhengyi, Yang Shuqing, He Yirong, and Lu Muwen, who were jointly responsible. In addition to their classes, they diligently guided the children in all aspects of their lives, including eating, sleeping, and bathing. Social activities were also managed by them. Lonely children gradually became familiar with their roommates and then expanded to a wider range. Outdoor walks, chats on the grass, (story time) after dinner, sports, gatherings, and trips all provided opportunities to practice socializing. I heard that many children cried when they first entered the camp because they were away from home, and one mother even cried after leaving her son. Now, this is no longer a problem, and they even prefer to stay in the camp. The child of that crying mother even sent a letter to comfort her. We know that most neurotic patients suffer from improper socialization, such as being ridiculed or scolded in front of others, liking this person and hating that person, or being intimidated, which can lead to future tragedies. A recent statistical report from the Ministry of Health stated that the number of people in our country who die from suicide and other abnormal causes reaches 6 million each year, with an estimated economic loss of 300 million yuan. Therefore, psychological hygiene in social interaction is particularly important in the camp. ▲Nutritional Attention: What we eat has a great impact on health and development. Since McColum woke people up, modern people have paid attention to experimental reports, which have been endless. For example, the difference between rats that eat milk and those that do not is extremely large. Those that eat milk develop quickly, have strong resistance, have a longer lifespan, and a lower mortality rate. After several generations, their physique is strong. Conversely, those that do not eat milk are not doing well. Now, our children are mostly thin and weak, short and feeble. Urban children eat too much meat, and rural children eat too many vegetables, neither of which is appropriate. Some children do not eat this or that, which also goes against nutritional principles. The health camp stipulates five meals a day. At 7:00 AM, there is porridge, noodles, or buttered bread, porridge and dishes, and rice and dishes are similar, avoiding salty things. At 10:00 AM, soy milk is given. Our country's soy milk is as nourishing as milk, cheap and beautiful. Schools and families should make children drink it often. At 12:00 PM, there is lunch. The menu changes daily, with a balanced mix of meat and vegetables. The main items are eggs, chicken, meat, fish, liver, blood, tofu, and green vegetables. At 4:00 PM, half a pound of milk is drunk, which Westerners call After School bile, which is also very important. At 7:00 PM, there is dinner, accompanied by mung bean porridge, red bean soup, noodles, and other items. After both lunch and dinner, various fruits such as oranges, apples, bananas, and hawthorns are served. The skins of hawthorns and other fruits are covered with bacteria, so they are washed and disinfected with one ten-thousandth (Potasu pcrmanganas) and cold boiled water. This kind of medicine costs about three or four cents a pound, and drugstores in Chengdu sell it. Schools and families can keep it on hand. Things grown on the ground have the most insects and bacteria. It is extremely dangerous to eat them without disinfection, and it seems that this can no longer be ignored. Watermelon is a heat-relieving food, and it is eaten several times a week. Children often reject cod liver oil. Dr. Wu Liguo of the Health Bureau used orange juice, lime, and malt extract to specially make a kind of liver oil for this camp. The results of the experiment were excellent. All the children in the camp accepted and swallowed it (color). After the camp is over, if they can continue to take it, the effect will be obvious. Their dining hall is simple and clean, with green oilcloth on the tables, two sets of sanitary spoons and chopsticks, and a plate. The red table indicates that you can take vegetables from the vegetable bowl to the rice bowl or plate. The blue table clearly indicates that private items can only be sent into the mouth. This sanitary usage prevents saliva from entering the vegetable bowl and prevents the spread of uncleanliness. The radio is turned on during meals to be fast and energetic. ▲Exercise Encouragement: Specially emphasizing eating and neglecting exercise is also not a way to health. Eating well also requires exercising well. They hold morning exercises at 7:00 AM and practice deep breathing. All teachers and students attend. At 11:00 AM, there is large muscle exercise, at 3:30 PM, there are games, from 4:20 PM to 5:00 PM, there are outdoor activities, from 5:00 PM to 7:00 PM, there is bathing, and before bed, there is massage. For the first three weeks of sunbathing, it is held at 9:00 AM every morning. For the last three weeks, morning exercises are changed to sunbathing exercises. Outdoor activities from 4:10 PM to 5:00 PM. The advantage of sunbathing and sunbathing exercises is that the ultraviolet light in the sun penetrates the skin, only penetrating to a thin layer of the skin, which is absorbed by the capillaries, increasing the speed of metabolism, making people have a good appetite and strong resistance. It's like adding new coal in the middle, making the fire burn and the heat increase. However, people with fever who are exposed to sunlight will burn even more severely, and there have been cases of people with lung disease dying from sun exposure. Therefore, children with fever cannot be exposed to sunlight. There is another type of child with yellow hair and brown eyes, which proves that their skin is fragile and cannot withstand too much sun exposure. They are prone to sun poisoning. The symptoms of poisoning include headache, insomnia, and irritability, starting with pus-filled blisters on the skin, and even death. For this type of child, each time can only be exposed for about five minutes, extending to about ten minutes. The sunbathing time for ordinary children should also be gradually increased. In the plains, start with five minutes and increase by one minute each day, up to twenty minutes or half an hour. Sunbathing once or once turning the skin black is harmful and useless. The skin becomes black, the cells die, and ultraviolet light cannot penetrate it. It is the same as not sunbathing, unless you wait until the skin peels off before proceeding. This camp pays close attention to these points for sunbathing and sunbathing exercises. They asked Dr. Gao Jinglang to select four children who could not be exposed to the sun and held separate classes. When exposed, they only wore a short pair of thin pants, their eyes were covered with black gauze, and their heads were also covered to prevent the sun from hurting their eyes and causing dizziness. Since the implementation, the results have been good, and the number of people with colds has decreased. Sports news.
